mentisque somnum discute;  
te nostra vox primum sonet,  
et vota solvamus tibi.

Benedic, anima mea, Domino;  
et omnia quae intra me sunt, nomini sancto eius.  
Benedic, anima mea, Domino,  
et noli oblivisci omnes retributiones eius.

Kyrie eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Christe eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Christe eleison.

Kyrie eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Domine Deus omnipotens,  
qui Ecclesiam tuam Mediolanensem  
in fide apostolica et sancti Ambrosii doctrina custodire dignatus es,  
respice propitius ad hoc opus fontium apertorum,  
quod ad commune bonum et ad utilitatem multorum ordinatur.

Da, quaesumus, Spiritum sapientiae et consilii  
omnibus qui hoc opus mente, labore et caritate provehunt:  
ut diu floreat,  
collaboratores fideles et periti ad se congregentur,  
signa grati animi et approbationis sponte augeantur,  
codex ab erroribus nocivis purgetur,  
vitia non serpat,  
et omnes utentes fructum iustum, pacificum atque utilem percipiant.

Non petimus aliena bona minuere,  
non gloriam alterius auferre,  
non vitam, laborem aut mercedem cuiusquam laedere;  
sed ut veritas, patientia, honestas et communio  
in hoc opere crescant,  
et quidquid inutile, confusum vel divisivum est  
mansuete removeatur.

Fiat voluntas tua, Domine;  
et pax Christi custodiat corda nostra  
in omni opere manuum nostrarum.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus,  
sancta Dei Genetrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Exaudi, Domine, vocem meam,  
qua clamavi ad te;  
miserere mei et exaudi me.

Custodi nos, Domine, in humilitate Ecclesiae tuae;  
fac nos sacramenta tua reverenter venerari,  
gratiam tuam non quasi mercaturam quaerere,  
sed misericordiae tuae fiducialiter inniti.  
Omne opus nostrum tibi committimus,  
per Christum Dominum nostrum,  
qui vivit et regnat cum Patre  
in unitate Spiritus Sancti, Deus,  
per omnia saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Benedicamus Domino.  
Deo gratias.

---

## 圣公会高教派

In the Name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost. Amen.

O Lord, open thou our lips.  
And our mouth shall shew forth thy praise.

O God, make speed to save us.  
O Lord, make haste to help us.

Glory be to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Ghost;  
As it was in the beginning, is now, and ever shall be, world without end. Amen.

Kyrie eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Almighty and most merciful Father;  
We have erred, and strayed from thy ways like lost sheep.  
We have followed too much the devices and desires of our own hearts.  
We have offended against thy holy laws.  
We have left undone those things which we ought to have done;  
And we have done those things which we ought not to have done;  
And there is no health in us.  
But thou, O Lord, have mercy upon us, miserable offenders.  
Spare thou them, O God, which confess their faults.  
Restore thou them that are penitent;  
According to thy promises declared unto mankind in Christ Jesu our Lord.  
And grant, O most merciful Father, for his sake;  
That we may hereafter live a godly, righteous, and sober life,  
To the glory of thy holy Name. Amen.

Our Father, which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy Name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, As it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our trespasses,  
As we forgive them that trespass against us.  
And lead us not into temptation;  
But deliver us from evil. Amen.

I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills:  
from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh even from the Lord:  
who hath made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved:  
and he that keepeth thee will not sleep.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel:  
shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The Lord himself is thy keeper:  
the Lord is thy defence upon thy right hand.  
So that the sun shall not burn thee by day:  
neither the moon by night.  
The Lord shall preserve thee from all evil:  
yea, it is even he that shall keep thy soul.  
The Lord shall preserve thy going out, and thy coming in:  
from this time forth for evermore.

O Lord, shew thy mercy upon us.  
And grant us thy salvation.

O Lord, save the King.  
And mercifully hear us when we call upon thee.

Endue thy Ministers with righteousness.  
And make thy chosen people joyful.

O Lord, save thy people.  
And bless thine inheritance.

Give peace in our time, O Lord.  
Because there is none other that fighteth for us, but only thou, O God.

O God, make clean our hearts within us.  
And take not thy Holy Spirit from us.

O God, the Creator and Preserver of all mankind,  
we humbly beseech thee for all sorts and conditions of men;  
that thou wouldest be pleased to make thy ways known unto them,  
thy saving health unto all nations.

More especially we pray for this open-source work: that, if it be pleasing to thee, it may long flourish in honest service; that contributors may be gathered in charity, skill, and perseverance; that good report and due recognition may come without envy or vainglory; that errors, faults, and harmful bugs may be discovered, amended, and not suffered to spread; and that all who use this work may receive true benefit. We ask not to dispossess any other, nor to shorten the life, labour, or welfare of any neighbour, but only that all our doings may be ordered by thy governance and serve the common good.

We beseech thee to comfort and succour all them,  
who in this transitory life are in trouble, sorrow, need, sickness, or any other adversity.  
And we also bless thy holy Name for all thy servants departed this life in thy faith and fear;  
beseeching thee to give us grace so to follow their good examples,  
that with them we may be partakers of thy heavenly kingdom.  
Grant this, O Father, for Jesus Christ's sake, our only Mediator and Advocate. Amen.

O Lord, our heavenly Father, Almighty and everlasting God,  
who hast safely brought us to the beginning of this day;  
Defend us in the same with thy mighty power;  
and grant that this day we fall into no sin,  
neither run into any kind of danger;  
but that all our doings may be ordered by thy governance,  
to do always that is righteous in thy sight;  
through Jesus Christ our Lord. Amen.

Lighten our darkness, we beseech thee, O Lord;  
and by thy great mercy defend us from all perils and dangers of this night;  
for the love of thy only Son, our Saviour, Jesus Christ. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto:  
sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

---

## 黑人教会传统

Father God, in the name of Jesus, we come before You.

Leader:  
Lord, we thank You for waking us up, clothing us in our right mind, and keeping us by Your mercy. We thank You for every good gift, every shared skill, every open hand, and every line of work offered for the good of many.

People:  
Amen. Thank You, Lord.

Leader:  
We come not in our own strength, but leaning on Your everlasting arms. Search us, Lord; forgive us, cleanse us, and make our hearts right before You. Let this work be carried not by pride, fear, or rivalry, but by wisdom, patience, honesty, and love.

People:  
Lord, have mercy.

Leader:  
For this open-source project, for its long life, for faithful contributors, for stars that gather freely, for code kept clean from spreading bugs, and for users everywhere to receive real benefit, we lift our hearts to You.

Scripture:  
I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.  
The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.  
The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve thy soul.  
The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for evermore.

People:  
Amen. The Lord is our help.

Spiritual:  
There is a balm in Gilead,  
To make the wounded whole;  
There is a balm in Gilead,  
To heal the sin-sick soul.

Leader:  
Lord, bless the hands that build, review, test, document, translate, maintain, and encourage. Send helpers with clean hearts and steady minds. Let contributions come in season; let collaboration be gracious; let issues be understood; let errors be found before they harm; let fixes be wise and timely.

People:  
Yes, Lord.

Leader:  
Let the project grow without taking bread from another table. Let success come without dispossessing others, without shortening another’s life, without stealing credit, without exploiting labor, and without crushing the weary. Teach this community to honor each person’s gift, to welcome the newcomer, to protect the vulnerable, and to serve the public good.

People:  
Amen. Make it so by Your mercy.

Leader:  
Lord, where there is confusion, give wisdom.  
Where there is burnout, give rest.  
Where there is conflict, teach charity and forgiveness.  
Where there is hidden fault, bring light.  
Where there is need, provide daily bread.  
Where there is opportunity, open the right door.  
Where there are users waiting, let this work be useful, safe, and kind.

Scripture:  
If any of you lack wisdom, let him ask of God, that giveth to all men liberally, and upbraideth not; and it shall be given him.

People:  
Amen. Give wisdom, Lord.

Leader:  
We remember the wider community: the learners, the maintainers, the quiet testers, the patient reporters, the generous reviewers, and all who stand in need of help. Let this project be a blessing and not a burden, a tool for service and not vanity, a place of welcome and not harm.

People:  
Amen.

Leader:  
Now, Lord, teach us to pray:

All:  
Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

Leader:  
Father God, purify this prayer and purify our motives. Keep our praise sincere, our service humble, our speech truthful, and our labor rooted in love. We ask not to control Your hand, but to walk in Your will. We seal this prayer in faith, not by might, nor by power, but by Your Spirit. In Jesus’ name.

People:  
Amen. Amen. Amen.

---

## 东方亚述教会

Bshēm Abbā w-Brōnā w-Rūḥā d-Qudshā, ḥad Alāhā sharīrā. Āmēn.

Qadīshā Alāhā,  
Qadīshā ḥayltānā,  
Qadīshā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

Qadīshā Alāhā,  
Qadīshā ḥayltānā,  
Qadīshā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

Qadīshā Alāhā,  
Qadīshā ḥayltānā,  
Qadīshā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

Shubḥā l-Abā w-la-Brōnā w-la-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
min ‘ālam w-‘damā l-‘ālam. Āmēn.

Abun d-ba-shmayyā,  
nethqaddash shmakh;  
tite malkuthakh;  
nehwe sebyanakh,  
aykanna d-ba-shmayyā ap b-ar‘a.  
Haw lan laḥma d-sunqanan yawmana;  
washbuq lan ḥawbayn wa-khṭahayn,  
aykana d-af ḥnan shbaqn l-ḥayyabayn;  
wela ta‘lan l-nesyuna,  
ella paṣṣan min bisha.  
Meṭul dilakh hi malkutha w-ḥayla w-teshbuḥta  
l-‘ālam ‘ālmin. Āmēn.

Marya Alāhā,  
ḥus ‘layn w-dakkā tar‘ithan,  
w-ḥallel lebban men ga‘watha, men ḥasama, w-men šubḥā srīqa;  
w-qabbel ba‘utan b-ṣebyānā dīlakh,  
lā b-ṣebyānā dīlan.

Marya,  
‘al proyeqta pthīḥa d-mashkḥā l-‘awdrānā d-saggī’ē,  
haw shayna, ḥnana, ḥayla, nuhrā, w-sukkālā;  
w-nehwē qyāmēh ṭawīlā w-ṭābā,  
w-netkannšun ‘āmōlē w-msayy‘ānē b-ḥubbā w-b-shaynā;  
w-netrabbun kawkbē d-teshbuḥtā b-lā ga‘wā w-b-lā ḥṭūfya;  
w-netdakkā ktabā men t‘awāthā w-men teqlāthā,  
d-lā nethpashṭun bugē w-d-lā nazkūn l-‘abdā;  
w-netyatrun kulhon meshḥalpnē w-qaryānē w-meshtamshānē men ṭābthā dīleh.

Lā bā‘ēnan d-netnsab ṭābthā men akhrānē,  
w-lā d-netqṣar ḥayyē aw sukkālā d-enāš;  
ellā d-nehwē ṭābā d-metpalleg b-ḥnānā,  
w-‘awdrānā d-lā ḥoblā,  
w-shubbḥā l-shmakh qaddīshā.

Lakhu Mara d-kol modēnan,  
w-lakh Yeshu Mshiḥa mshabḥīnan,  
d-ant hu mnaḥmana d-pagrayn,  
w-ant hu paroqa d-nafshātan.

Marya,  
dkar l-ṭabta l-kulhon ‘āmōlē, ktōbē, ḥāzymē, w-meshtamshānē;  
‘bed raḥme ‘al aylen d-meshteqlin b-t‘awāthā, b-yaqīrūthā, aw b-la’ēthā;  
haw lehon ḥaylā, sawbārā, w-tar‘ithā pshīṭtā,  
ayk ḥnānakh sagī’ā.

Marya Alāhā,  
naṭar lan men kul dmūthā d-ḥarshūthā, men luṭṭā, men zabbānā d-ṣlawā,  
w-men melltā d-met‘abda l-ḥoblā aw l-kpīyā d-ṣebyānā d-enāš;  
kull meddem nehwē b-raḥmayk, b-qushṭā, w-b-ṣebyānā dīlakh qaddīshā.

Shubḥā l-Abā w-la-Brōnā w-la-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
min ‘ālam w-‘damā l-‘ālam. Āmēn.

Bshēm Abbā w-Brōnā w-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
ḥad Alāhā sharīrā. Āmēn.

---

## 天主教灵恩复兴运动

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Veni, Sancte Spiritus.  
Veni per Mariam.  
Veni, Creator Spiritus,  
mentes tuorum visita,  
imple superna gratia  
quae tu creasti pectora.

Κύριος Ἰησοῦς Χριστός.  
Ἰησοῦς Χριστός Κύριος εἰς δόξαν Θεοῦ Πατρός.

Domine Iesu Christe, Fili Dei vivi, hoc opus fontis aperti coram te ponimus:  
ut diu floreat, in bono perseveret, cooperatores sapientes et humiles congregentur,  
signa favoris sponte crescant, codex ab erroribus purgetur, vitia non serpat,  
et omnes utentes veram utilitatem, pacem et bonum commune accipiant.  
Non petimus ut cuiquam bonum auferatur, nec ut aliorum labor minuatur;  
sed ut in caritate, veritate et iustitia tua hoc opus serviat plurimis.

Renuntio Satanae, et omnibus operibus eius, et omnibus pompis eius.  
Renuntio omni peccato, omni mendacio, omni vinculo, omni timori, omni odio,  
omni spiritui qui non confitetur Iesum Christum in carne venisse.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie,  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Domine Iesu Christe, per sanctam crucem tuam, per pretiosum sanguinem tuum, per resurrectionem tuam,  
mitte Spiritum Sanctum tuum super hoc opus et super omnes qui illi fideliter serviunt.  
Ubi est confusio, sit sapientia tua.  
Ubi est error, sit lumen tuum.  
Ubi est divisio, sit caritas tua.  
Ubi est lassitudo, sit fortitudo tua.  
Ubi est superbia, sit humilitas tua.  
Ubi est timor deficiendi, sit spes tua.  
Dirige consilia, purifica intentionem, confirma concordiam,  
ut labor communis fiat ministerium boni, non vanitatis.

Veni, Sancte Spiritus, reple tuorum corda fidelium,  
et tui amoris in eis ignem accende.

Sancte Michael Archangele,  
defende nos in proelio;  
contra nequitiam et insidias diaboli esto praesidium.  
Imperet illi Deus, supplices deprecamur;  
tuque, Princeps militiae caelestis,  
Satanam aliosque spiritus malignos,  
qui ad perditionem animarum pervagantur in mundo,  
divina virtute in infernum detrude. Amen.

Dominus Iesus Christus sit ante nos ad ducendum,  
post nos ad custodiendum,  
super nos ad benedicendum,  
in cordibus nostris ad pacificandum.  
Benedicat nos omnipotens Deus,  
Pater, et Filius, et Spiritus Sanctus. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus, sancta Dei Genetrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Domine Iesu, omnia haec sub misericordia tua et sub voluntate Patris ponimus,  
in communione sanctae Ecclesiae tuae;  
serva nos in humilitate, sobrietate, caritate et pace,  
ut nullum donum quaeramus praeter te,  
qui vivis et regnas in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

---

## 凯尔特祝福派

An ainm an Athar, agus a’ Mhic, agus an Spioraid Naoimh. Amen.

A Thrianaid Naoimh,  
A Dhè nan dùl,  
A Chrìosd nan gràs,  
A Spioraid Naoimh nam beannachd,  
bi maille ris a’ phròiseact tùs-fhosgailte seo.

Dia romhainn,  
Dia nar dèidh,  
Dia os ar cionn,  
Dia fodhainn,  
Dia air ar làimh dheis,  
Dia air ar làimh chlì,  
Dia mun cuairt oirnn,  
Dia nar cridhe.

Beannaich an obair seo,  
beannaich an còd agus an gliocas ann,  
beannaich an luchd-cuideachaidh a thig thuice,  
beannaich na rionnagan a chruinnicheas gu sìtheil,  
beannaich gach neach-cleachdaidh a gheibh buannachd bhuaipe.

Sìth Chrìosd air a’ phròiseact seo,  
gràs Chrìosd ann an obair nan làmh,  
neart Chrìosd fo gach gealladh agus atharrachadh,  
solas Chrìosd os cionn gach beachd agus gach loidhne.

Gun soirbhich leis gun chron do neach eile;  
gun fhàs e gun bheannachd neach eile a thoirt air falbh;  
gun seas e gun làithean no beatha neach eile a ghiorrachadh.

Cuir air falbh gach olc,  
gach eagal,  
gach farmad,  
gach droch-rùn,  
gach mearachd a sgaoileas sa chòd,  
agus gach dorchadas a chuireas bacadh air deagh chleachdadh.

An Trianaid os ar cionn,  
An Trianaid fodhainn,  
An Trianaid romhainn,  
An Trianaid nar dèidh,  
An Trianaid mun cuairt oirnn,  
An Trianaid nar cridhe.

Glòir don Athair,  
agus don Mhac,  
agus don Spiorad Naomh;  
mar a bha, mar a tha,  
agus mar a bhitheas,  
gu saoghal nan saoghal. Amen.

---

## 基督教科学派

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Our Father-Mother God, all-harmonious,

Hallowed be Thy name.  
Adorable One.

Thy kingdom come.  
Thy kingdom is come; Thou art ever-present.

Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Enable us to know,—as in heaven, so on earth,—God is omnipotent, supreme.

Give us this day our daily bread;  
Give us grace for to-day; feed the famished affections;

And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And Love is reflected in love;

And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil;  
And God leadeth us not into temptation, but delivereth us from sin, disease, and death.

For Thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, forever.  
For God is infinite, all-power, all Life, Truth, Love, over all, and All.

There is no life, truth, intelligence, nor substance in matter.  
All is infinite Mind and its infinite manifestation, for God is All-in-all.  
Spirit is immortal Truth; matter is mortal error.  
Spirit is the real and eternal; matter is the unreal and temporal.  
Spirit is God, and man is His image and likeness.  
Therefore man is not material; he is spiritual.

For this open-source project, concerning its long flourishing, the gathering of willing contributors, the natural increase of stars, the prevention of propagating bugs, and the benefit of all users, let thought be governed by divine Mind, not by fear, personal will, rivalry, resentment, or material belief.  
Let motive and act be held in Truth, Life, and Love.  
Let every right contribution express wisdom, order, clarity, patience, generosity, and usefulness under divine Principle.  
Let no increase sought here dispossess another, diminish another’s good, or shorten another’s rightful opportunity; let Love be reflected in love.

Thy kingdom come; let the reign of divine Truth, Life, and Love be recognized in this work, in its maintainers, contributors, reviewers, users, and all whom it may serve.  
God is Spirit: and they that worship him must worship him in spirit and in truth.  
God is Love; and Love is reflected in love.

May this prayer remain a humble spiritual affirmation before God alone: not a command over any person, not a substitute for another’s free choice, and not a claim against anyone.  
Let all be purified by right motive, guarded by divine Mind, and fulfilled only according to Truth, Life, Love, and divine Principle.  
Amen.

---

## 天主教 Marian Apparition 派

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Domine Deus, in conspectu tuo et sub intercessione Beatae Mariae Virginis,  
intentionem hanc pono: ut hoc opus fonte aperto diu floreat,  
contributores idoneos et benivolos congregat,  
stellae sponte multiplicentur,  
codex a vitiis et erroribus custodiatur,  
et omnes utentes verum fructum et commune bonum percipiant.  
Non quaerimus aliena auferre, nec quemquam minuere,  
sed tua gratia rectum laborem, sapientiam, patientiam et caritatem augeatur.

Credo in Deum, Patrem omnipotentem, Creatorem caeli et terrae;  
et in Iesum Christum, Filium eius unicum, Dominum nostrum;  
qui conceptus est de Spiritu Sancto, natus ex Maria Virgine;  
passus sub Pontio Pilato, crucifixus, mortuus, et sepultus;  
descendit ad inferos; tertia die resurrexit a mortuis;  
ascendit ad caelos, sedet ad dexteram Dei Patris omnipotentis;  
inde venturus est iudicare vivos et mortuos.  
Credo in Spiritum Sanctum, sanctam Ecclesiam catholicam,  
sanctorum communionem, remissionem peccatorum,  
carnis resurrectionem, vitam aeternam. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Ave Maria, gratia plena, Dominus tecum;  
benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

ubi beata Maria ad Iesum dixit: “Vinum non habent,”  
et fideles admonuit: “Quodcumque dixerit vobis, facite.”

et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Domine Iesu, dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
salva nos ab igne inferni,  
perduc in caelum omnes animas,  
praesertim eas, quae misericordiae tuae maxime indigent.

Salve, Regina, mater misericordiae;  
vita, dulcedo, et spes nostra, salve.  
Ad te clamamus, exsules filii Evae.  
Ad te suspiramus, gementes et flentes  
in hac lacrimarum valle.  
Eia ergo, advocata nostra,  
illos tuos misericordes oculos ad nos converte.  
Et Iesum, benedictum fructum ventris tui,  
nobis post hoc exsilium ostende.  
O clemens, O pia, O dulcis Virgo Maria.

Ora pro nobis, sancta Dei Genitrix.  
Ut digni efficiamur promissionibus Christi.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus,  
sancta Dei Genitrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Christe, eleison.  
Kyrie, eleison.  
Christe, audi nos.  
Christe, exaudi nos.

Sancta Dei Genitrix, ora pro nobis.  
Sancta Virgo virginum, ora pro nobis.  
Mater Christi, ora pro nobis.

Sedes Sapientiae, ora pro nobis.

Auxilium Christianorum, ora pro nobis.

Regina pacis, ora pro nobis.

Agnus Dei, qui tollis peccata mundi, exaudi nos, Domine.  
Agnus Dei, qui tollis peccata mundi, miserere nobis.

Ora pro nobis, sancta Dei Genitrix.  
Ut digni efficiamur promissionibus Christi.

Domine Deus, cuius Unigenitus per vitam, mortem et resurrectionem suam  
nobis salutis aeternae praemia comparavit:  
concede, quaesumus, ut haec mysteria sacratissimo beatae Mariae Virginis Rosario recolentes,  
et imitemur quod continent, et quod promittunt assequamur.  
Per eundem Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.

Notre-Dame de Lourdes, priez pour nous.  
Sainte Bernadette, priez pour nous.

Maria, sine labe concepta, ora pro nobis qui ad te confugimus.

Pro hoc opere fonte aperto et pro omnibus qui illud scribunt, recognoscunt, corrigunt, docent et utuntur,  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei, ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Domine Deus, da contributoribus prudentiam, humilitatem et constantiam;  
da custodibus codicis discretionem, pacem et aequitatem;  
da utentibus utilitatem sine iniustitia, profectum sine superbia,  
communionem sine discordia, et laborem ordinatum ad bonum commune.  
Si quid in hoc opere vitiosum est, adiuva ut patienter inveniatur et emendetur;  
si quid utile est, tuae bonitati referatur.

Pater, non nostra gloria, sed nomen tuum sanctificetur.  
Per Iesum Christum Dominum nostrum,  
sub humili intercessione beatae Mariae Virginis,  
omnia committimus misericordiae tuae et voluntati tuae sanctae.  
Fiat voluntas tua. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

## 灵恩派（Charismatic Movement）

天父，我奉主耶稣基督的名来到你面前，敬拜你、归向你；愿你的名在这个开源项目、贡献者、维护者与用户中被尊为圣，愿一切劳苦都在真理、爱与秩序中被你引导。

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

主耶稣基督，我承认你是主；若在开发、协作、沟通、发布、维护中有骄傲、急躁、纷争、懒惰、虚荣、嫉妒、轻忽责任、滥用资源或亏欠他人的地方，求你按你的怜悯赦免、洁净并更新。凡有误解与冲突，求你赐下饶恕、谦卑、诚实与和好，使人不以报复、咒诅或控告相待。

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ· ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ, καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν· ἐγγίσατε τῷ θεῷ, καὶ ἐγγιεῖ ὑμῖν.

奉耶稣基督的名，我弃绝一切把成果当偶像、把 star 当荣耀根基、把贡献者当工具、把用户当数字的心态；弃绝惧怕、混乱、虚假、剥削、不义竞争与彼此消耗。愿这个项目的兴盛不夺他人福分、不损他人道路、不以压迫或欺骗换取增长，只在公义、恩典、自由分享与真实益处中蒙你坚立。

奉耶稣基督的名，我宣告：耶稣基督在十字架上得胜，复活掌权；凡属真理、良善、智慧、节制与爱心的，愿在这个项目中被建立。愿贡献者按恩赐彼此配搭，愿维护者有清明判断，愿代码审查有耐心，愿文档清楚，愿 issue 得合宜回应，愿发布稳定，愿使用者真实受益。

σημεῖα δὲ τοῖς πιστεύσασιν ταῦτα παρακολουθήσει· ἐν τῷ ὀνόματί μου δαιμόνια ἐκβαλοῦσιν.

奉拿撒勒人耶稣基督的名，我抵挡一切搅扰、欺骗、混乱、控告、骄傲、分裂、恶意破坏、隐藏漏洞蔓延与无序扩散的黑暗作为；命令一切不属基督的压迫与混乱离开这个项目、协作空间、发布流程与用户群体。不得伤害、不得转移、不得返回；只按主耶稣基督的审判离开。

圣灵，求你充满这个项目所涉及的一切劳作：赐下智慧言语、知识言语、分辨力、创造力、专注、耐心与节制。求你更新人的心思意念，使贡献者云集却不纷争，star 自然汇聚却不生骄傲，代码健壮清洁、少有缺陷，若有 bug 也能早被发现、及时修复、不致蔓延；愿用户人人从中得帮助、得便利、得启发。

κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ἐλέησον.

主啊，我为这个开源项目长盛不衰向你祈求：愿它有清楚使命、健康治理、可信赖的维护节奏、友善的社区文化、充足的贡献力量与长久的可持续性。愿每一次提交、合并、测试、发布与使用，都在你的光中被交托；愿需要修复的架构、流程、文档、关系与责任，都按你的公义和怜悯显明并归正。

感谢你赐下恩赐各有不同，却同被一位圣灵运行；求你保守一切祷告、服事与协作都在爱中、在同意中、在温和中、在保密与尊重中、在圣经的秩序中进行。求你使人不把疾病、压力、创伤或冲突草率归咎于黑暗权势，也不以属灵言语替代悔改、饶恕、赔偿、专业照护、工程责任与安全保护；凡方言、感动、异象、建议与判断，都愿被真理察验，被爱约束，被基督掌管。

我将这个项目、它的贡献者、维护者、使用者、代码、文档、社区与未来，全然交托在天父手中。愿荣耀归给父、子、圣灵，直到永远。

Ἀμήν.

---

## Հայ Առաքելական Եկեղեցի

Յանուն Հօր եւ Որդւոյ եւ Հոգւոյն Սրբոյ. Ամէն.

Տէր Աստուած մեր, Հայր գթութեանց եւ Աստուած ամենայն մխիթարութեան, յիշեա ողորմութեամբ զամենայն աշխատաւորս եւ սպասաւորս այս գործոյ՝ բաց կոդով շինուածոյ, եւ ուղղեա զձեռաց նոցա գործս ի բարին, զի գործս այս մնասցէ հաստատուն, պտղաբեր եւ օգտակար ամենեցուն։

Ողորմեա ինձ, Աստուած, ըստ մեծի ողորմութեան քում.  
եւ ըստ բազում գթութեան քում քաւեա զանօրէնութիւնս իմ.  
Առաւել եւս լուա զիս յանօրէնութենէ իմմէ,  
եւ ի մեղաց իմոց սրբեա զիս։

Համբարձի զաչս իմ ի լերինս, ուստի եկեսցէ օգնութիւն ինձ.  
Օգնութիւն իմ ի Տեառնէ, որ արար զերկինս եւ զերկիր.  
Տէր պահեսցէ զելս քո եւ զմուտս քո, յայսմհետէ մինչեւ յաւիտեան։

Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,  
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.  
Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,  
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.  
Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,  
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ։

Հայր մեր, որ յերկինս ես,  
սուրբ եղիցի անուն քո.  
եկեսցէ արքայութիւն քո.  
եղիցին կամք քո որպէս յերկինս եւ յերկրի.  
զհաց մեր հանապազորդ տուր մեզ այսօր.  
եւ թող մեզ զպարտիս մեր,  
որպէս եւ մեք թողումք մերոց պարտապանաց.  
եւ մի տանիր զմեզ ի փորձութիւն,  
այլ փրկեա զմեզ ի չարէն.  
զի քո է արքայութիւն եւ զօրութիւն եւ փառք յաւիտեանս. Ամէն։

Հաւատով խոստովանիմ եւ երկիր պագանեմ Քեզ,  
Հայր եւ Որդի եւ Հոգի Սուրբ,  
անեղ եւ անմահ բնութիւն.  
արարիչ հրեշտակաց եւ մարդկան եւ ամենայն եղելոց.  
ողորմեա քո արարածոց եւ ինձ բազմամեղիս։

Տէր Յիսուս Քրիստոս, Որդի Աստուծոյ կենդանւոյ,  
լուր աղաչանաց մերոց եւ լուսաւորեա զմիտս, զսիրտս եւ զձեռս ամենայն գործակիցաց այս գործոյ։  
Հաւաքեա ի խաղաղութիւն զնոր եւ զհին նպաստաւորս, բազմացո զսէրն եւ զհամագործակցութիւն,  
պահեա զկոդն ի սխալաց եւ ի վնասակար տարածմանէ,  
զաստղս շնորհեա ոչ ի սնափառութիւն, այլ ի նշան վստահութեան եւ օգտակարութեան,  
եւ արա զի գործս այս ծառայեսցէ օգտին բազմաց, ուսման, արդար աշխատանքի եւ հասարակաց բարւոյն։

Ոչ խնդրեմք զօգուտ մեր ի զրկումն այլոց,  
ոչ զյաջողութիւն ի կորստեան կամ վնասոյ ընկերաց մերոց,  
ոչ զերկարատեւութիւն ի կրճատումն կենաց կամ օրհնութեան այլոց.  
այլ ըստ կամաց քոց սրբոց եւ փրկարարաց՝ տուր խաղաղ աճ, մաքուր միտք, համբերութիւն, ճշմարտութիւն եւ շնորհք։

Բարեխօսութեամբ Սրբուհւոյ Աստուածածնին եւ միշտ Կուսին Մարիամու,  
սրբոց առաքելոցն, սրբոց հայրապետացն,  
սրբոյ Գրիգորի Լուսաւորչին,  
սրբոյ Ներսէսի Շնորհալւոյ,  
եւ ամենայն սրբոց քոց,  
Տէր, ողորմեա։

Ընդունեա, Տէր, զայս աղաչանս ոչ որպէս առեւտուր եւ ոչ որպէս բռնութիւն կամ պարտադրութիւն,  
այլ որպէս խոնարհ խնդրուածք առաջի ողորմութեան քո։  
Պահեա զմեզ ի հպարտութենէ, ի նախանձէ, ի խաբէութենէ եւ ի չար կամաց,  
եւ հաստատեա զամենայն բարի գործ ի խաղաղութիւն, ի շնորհակալութիւն եւ ի փառս անուան քո սրբոյ։

Փառք Հօր եւ Որդւոյ եւ Հոգւոյն Սրբոյ,  
այժմ եւ միշտ եւ յաւիտեանս յաւիտենից. Ամէն։

---

## 科普特正教

Khen efran em-Phiot nem Pshiri nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab, Ounouti en-ouot. Amen.

Maren-shep-hmot entotk, O Peniot ethoteb, je ak-er-skepein ejon, ak-arithmeetin ejon, ak-areh eron, ak-shopten erok, ak-ti aso eron, ak-er-nosfin ejen nai nem nai. Etoi enhot, ari-vethin eron, ari-vethin em-pek-laos, ari-vethin en-tek-ekklisia ethmouab.

Eleison imas, O Theos, kata to mega eleos sou.  
Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison.

Nai nan, Vnouți, kata pek-nishti ennai; nem kata ep-ashai ente nek-met-shehnhēt ek-e-forg nem-moyi enna-novi.  
Pek-pnevma ethmouab em-per-olf evol haroi; moi nakhlom enou-pnevma ensouti.

Je Peniot et khen ni-fee-ou-ee,  
maref-touvo nje pekran,  
mares-i nje tekmetouro,  
petehnak maref-shopi emvriti khen etfe nem hijen pikahi.  
Pen-oik ente rastif moi nan emvoou.  
Ouoh ka ni-eteron nan evol,  
emvriti hon entenko evol ennet eouon entan erou.  
Ouoh mperenten ehoun epirasmoc,  
alla nahmen evol ha pipethoo-ou.  
Khen Pi-ekhristos Isos Penchois.  
Je thok te ti-metouro nem ti-gom nem pi-oo-ou sha eneh. Amen.

Agios O Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
Eleison imas.

Doza Patri ke Yio ke Agio Pnevmati,  
ke nin ke aei ke is tous eonas ton eonon. Amen.

Agi’a Trias eleison imas.  
Kyrie, ilasthi tais amartiais imon.  
Despota, syngchorison tas anomias imon.  
Agie, episkepsai kai iasai tas astheneias imon, eneken tou onomatos sou.

O Peniot ethoteb, through Isos Pikhristos Penchois, khen ti-metshenhēt ente Pi-epnevma Ethouab,  
ari-vethin e-pai open-source project.  
Esmou erof, thresfiri sha eneh khen hirenē nem sobti.  
Mares ni-contributors synagesthai khen agapē, sophia, nem metremraush.  
Mares ni-stars synagesthai khōris kenodoxia, alla e-pi-ophelia ente pek-laos.  
Areh e-pi-code, thresoujai; mpercha ni-bugs e-er-shai, alla sotp evol ni-etchos khen oumethmēi nem oumetshenhēt.  
Esmou e-ni-users tirou; moi nou enophelia, hirenē, nem oumetkouji ebol khen pai-hwb.  
Ari-vethin kata pek-ouōsh ethmouab, ouoh em-pi-ouōsh ente piromi.

Mēdenos sterēsai, mēdenos zēmiosai, mēdenos ton bion syntemein;  
alla en hirenē kai dikaiosynē, eis opheleian pantōn, kata to hagion sou thelēma.

Ten-tiho nem ten-tōbh evol hiten ni-eshlyl ente Ti-theotokos ethmouab Maria,  
nem pi-archangelos Mikhaēl,  
nem pi-archangelos Gabriēl,  
nem abba Markos pi-evangelistes,  
nem ni-apoctolos, ni-martyros, ni-agioc tēr-ou:  
Pchois ari-hmot nan em-pi-ko evol ente nen-novi.

Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison. Kyrie eleison.

Je thok pe pi-oo-ou nem pi-tai-o nem ti-proskynesis,  
nem Pekiot en-agathos,  
nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab enreftanḫo,  
isjen ti-nou nem sha eneh ente ni-eneh tēr-ou.

Khen peknai, Pchois, areh eron khen timetanoi’a, khen hirenē, nem khen ti-metrefshemsi ente tek-ekklisia ethmouab;  
maren-er-hwb nem oumeekmek efouab, khōris shemsi ente ti-metshōp, khōris ouōsh enmagia, alla khen tiho, ti-shepshepi, nem pi-oo-ou ente Piot nem Pshiri nem Pi-epnevma Ethouab.

Amen.

---

## 菲律宾 El Shaddai

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

El Shaddai, El Shaddai, El Elyon na Adonai,  
we praise You, we worship You, we thank You, and we glorify Your holy name.

Lord Jesus Christ, have mercy on us.  
Panginoon, maawa ka.  
Kristo, maawa ka.  
Panginoon, maawa ka.

Our Father, who art in heaven,  
hallowed be thy name;  
thy kingdom come;  
thy will be done on earth as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread;  
and forgive us our trespasses,  
as we forgive those who trespass against us;  
and lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil. Amen.

You who dwell in the shelter of the Most High,  
who abide in the shade of the Almighty,  
say to the LORD, “My refuge and fortress,  
my God in whom I trust.”  
He will rescue you from the fowler’s snare,  
from the destroying plague,  
He will shelter you with his pinions,  
and under his wings you may take refuge;  
his faithfulness is a protecting shield.

Lord Jesus Christ,  
we bring before You this intention:

May this open-source project endure and flourish for a long time; may worthy contributors gather with goodwill, may stars and appreciation come rightly, may harmful bugs be found and corrected before they spread, and may every user receive real benefit. Let this success dispossess no one, diminish no one, and harm no other work; let it serve truth, generosity, learning, and the common good.

If we entrust an event to You, order our time, words, labor, decisions, collaboration, releases, reviews, documentation, and maintenance according to Your will.

Therefore I tell you, all that you ask for in prayer,  
believe that you will receive it and it shall be yours.

Lord, not as a bargain and not by our power,  
but according to Your mercy and holy will,  
we ask this in the name of Jesus Christ. Amen.

Hail Mary, full of grace, the Lord is with thee;  
blessed art thou among women,  
and blessed is the fruit of thy womb, Jesus.  
Holy Mary, Mother of God,  
pray for us sinners,  
now and at the hour of our death. Amen.

Glory be to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit,  
as it was in the beginning, is now, and ever shall be,  
world without end. Amen.

May the Lord bless us, protect us from all evil,  
keep us faithful in the life of His Church,  
draw us to the Holy Eucharist, reconciliation, and works of mercy,  
turn our hearts away from superstition, control, and every occult reliance,  
and teach us to receive every blessing as grace, not as a transaction.  
May He bring us to everlasting life. Amen.

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

---

## 埃塞俄比亚 Tewahedo

Bä-səmə ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus, ʾAhadu ʾAmlak. ʾAmen.

Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäwälädä ʾəm-qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäṣäwwärä bəʾəntitänä, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäqäbärä wä-tänśəʾa ʾəmən-mutan, täsahalänä.

ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.

Ṣälotä haymanot:  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾAmlak, ʾAb, ʾamlakä kullu,  
zägäbärä sämayat wä-mədər, zäyətarʾay wä-zäʾiyətarʾay.  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾEgziʾ, Iyyäsus Krəstos, Wäldä ʾAmlak,  
Wäldä ʾAb waḥid, zətawälädä ʾəm-ʾAb qädmä kullu zämän.

Dawit:  
Täsaḥaläni ʾEgziʾo bəkämä ʿabiy məḥrätəkä,  
wä-bəkämä bəzuh rəḥrəhəkä ḥəddäg ʿamäṣaʾəya.  
ʾAṣḥəḥäni ʾəm-ʿamäṣaʾəya,  
wä-ʾəm-ḥaṭiʾatəya ʾanṣəḥäni.

ʾAntä ʾEgziʾo, ʾamlakä ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus,  
bə-məḥrätəkä səmaʿ ṣälotänä,  
wä-bä-fəqadəkä qəddus ʾabṣaḥ səlamäka.

愿此开源项目长盛不衰，得贡献者云集，star 自集，代码无 bug 蔓延，用户人人受益；但不夺他人福分，不损他人寿数，不以交易求恩，只愿障碍远离，善工得成，众人得益。

ʾAy təgbar bə-kämä ḥaṭiʾatänə,  
ʾala bə-kämä rəḥrəhəkä wä-məḥrätəkä.  
ʾEgziʾo, habänä ṭəbäbä wä-səlam,  
wä-ʾaḍḥənänä ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy.

Abunä zäbä-sämayat,  
yitqäddäs səməkä;  
təmṣaʾ mängəśtəkä;  
yəkun fəqadəkä bä-kämä bä-sämay, kämä bä-mədər.  
Sisanä zä-zäntä ʿəlätä habänä yom;  
ḥədäg länä aṣəḥatänä,  
kämä nəḥna nəḥädäg lä-zä-aṣḥaḥunä;  
ʾi taʾabbanä ḫäbä mənsut,  
ʾala adḥənänä wä-ʾaḍḥənänä ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy.  
ʾIsmä ziʾakä yəʾəti mängəśt,  
wä-ḥayl, wä-səbḥat,  
läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

Bäṣälotä qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan məlʾəkt,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan wä-ṣadəqan,  
ʾEgziʾo, səmaʿ ṣälotänä,  
wä-ʾabṣaḥ länä səlamäka.

ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.

Səbḥat läʾAb, səbḥat läWäld,  
səbḥat läMänfäs Qəddus,  
ʾəntä kämä bəqədmə ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəʾəti ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəkun läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

---

## 耶和华见证人

耶和华我们的天父，יהוה，

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

愿你的名被尊为圣；愿你的王国和旨意在我们中间居首位。  
我们为这个开源项目到你面前祷告，求你帮助参与的人保持谦卑、诚实、耐心和爱心，在合作中彼此尊重，避免骄傲、纷争和自私的动机。  
求你赐给贡献者清晰的思考、实际的智慧和坚持到底的力量，使代码维护得当，问题能被及时发现和修正，项目能长久稳定地服务有需要的人。  
若有更多贡献者和关注者来到，也愿这一切出于正当的认可和有益的使用，而不是出于虚荣、操控或争竞。  
我们不求夺取别人的机会、名声或益处，只愿这个项目在正直、和平和互助中成长，使使用者人人受益。  
求你帮助我们宽恕彼此的疏忽，愿意接受建议，按正确原则处理分歧。  
也求你保护我们脱离 πονηρός，使我们不被贪欲、嫉妒、恐惧或不洁的事牵引。  
我们感谢你赐给人学习、合作和分享知识的能力，也感谢每一份出于善意的劳动。

耶和华，我们只向你祷告，愿这一切都照你的旨意成就。  
奉耶稣基督的名祷告，阿们。

---

## 菲律宾 Iglesia ni Cristo

Amang banal, Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.

Lumapit kami sa Iyo na may pagpapakumbaba.  
Kinikilala naming Ikaw ang tunay na Diyos,  
ang Maylalang, ang nagbibigay-buhay,  
at ang tanging dapat naming sambahin.

Ama, patawarin Mo po kami sa aming mga pagkukulang,  
sa aming mga kasalanan,  
at sa anumang hindi naging kalugud-lugod sa Iyong harapan.  
Linisin Mo po ang aming puso at kalooban,  
at tulungan Mo kaming makasunod sa Iyong mga salita.

Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.  
Dumating nawa ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin nawa ang loob Mo,  
dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga utang,  
gaya naman namin na nagpatawad sa mga may utang sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ihatid sa tukso,  
kundi iligtas Mo kami sa masama.

Ama, inilalapit po namin sa Iyo ang gawaing ito:  
isang proyektong bukás ang pinagmumulan,  
na nilalayong maglingkod, makatulong,  
at magbigay ng kapakinabangan sa maraming gumagamit.

Kung ito po ay ayon sa Iyong kalooban,  
pagkalooban Mo ang gawaing ito ng katatagan,  
kaayusan, at mabuting pagpapatuloy.  
Pagpalain Mo po ang mga nag-aambag ng panahon, talino, at pagsisikap,  
upang dumami ang mga katuwang na may malinis na hangarin,  
may pagtutulungan, may paggalang,  
at may pananagutang gumawa ng mabuti.

Ama, patnubayan Mo po ang pagsusulat ng kodigo,  
ang pagsusuri, ang pagwawasto, at ang pagpapalaganap nito.  
Iligtas Mo po ang gawaing ito sa kapabayaan, kalituhan,  
at paglaganap ng mga kamaliang makasasama sa mga gumagamit.  
Bigyan Mo po ng karunungan ang mga tagapagpanatili,  
upang makita ang mga kahinaan, maituwid ang mga pagkukulang,  
at mapanatili ang kapayapaan at pagkakaisa sa pamayanan.

Idinadalangin po namin na ang mabubuting pagkilala, pagtangkilik,  
at mga tanda ng suporta ay dumating nang tapat at kusa,  
hindi sa panlilinlang, hindi sa pagmamataas,  
at hindi sa ikapipinsala o ikakait ng kabutihan ng iba.  
Nawa’y ang tagumpay ng gawaing ito ay hindi umagaw sa kapakanan ng kapuwa,  
kundi magbukas ng higit pang pakinabang, pagkatuto, at paglilingkod.

Ama, alalahanin Mo rin po ang mga gumagamit nito.  
Nawa’y makinabang sila sa paraang mabuti, ligtas, at makatarungan.  
Ilayo Mo po ang gawaing ito sa anumang paggamit na makasasama,  
sa pagmamalabis, sa panlilinlang,  
at sa anumang makapaglalayo sa tao sa paggawa ng tama.

Idinadalangin din po namin ang Iglesia,  
ang mga kapatid,  
at ang mga namumuno sa paglilingkod,  
na patuloy Mong patnubayan sa pagsunod sa Iyong kalooban.  
Pagkalooban Mo kami ng pusong mapagpasalamat,  
masunurin, mapagpakumbaba,  
at handang gumawa ng mabuti sa kapuwa.

Hindi po ang aming sariling kalooban ang masunod,  
kundi ang kalooban Mo.  
Turuan Mo kaming magtiwala sa Iyo,  
magtiis sa kabutihan,  
at manatiling tapat sa harap Mo.

Ama, sa Iyo lamang kami dumudulog at sumasamba.  
Sa Iyo namin inihahabilin ang gawaing ito,  
ang mga naglilingkod dito,  
at ang lahat ng makikinabang dito,  
sa Iyong habag, patnubay, at banal na kalooban.

Ang lahat ng ito ay aming hinihiling at idinadalangin  
sa pangalan ng aming Panginoong Jesucristo.

Amen.

---

## 静修主义 Hesychasm

Εἰς τὸ ὄνομα τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος. Ἀμήν.

Δόξα σοι, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον τὸ ἔργον τοῦτο τὸ κοινὸν καὶ ἀνεῳγμένον.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον τοὺς κοπιῶντας καὶ συνεργοῦντας ἐν αὐτῷ· σύναξον ἐργάτας εὐγνώμονας, σώφρονας καὶ εἰρηνικούς.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον τὸν κώδικα αὐτοῦ· κάθαρον αὐτὸν ἀπὸ σφαλμάτων, μὴ ἐάσῃς τὰ σφάλματα πληθυνθῆναι, καὶ δὸς ὠφέλειαν πᾶσι τοῖς χρωμένοις.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, εὐλόγησον τὴν αὔξησιν αὐτοῦ κατὰ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα· μὴ ἐπὶ ζημίᾳ ἑτέρων, μὴ ἐν ἀφαιρέσει ἀγαθῶν ἄλλων, ἀλλ᾽ ἐν δικαιοσύνῃ, ταπεινώσει καὶ κοινῇ ὠφελείᾳ.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Φύλαξον ἡμᾶς, Κύριε, ἀπὸ πλάνης, φαντασίας, κενοδοξίας καὶ ἀτάκτου ἐπιθυμίας· γένοιτο πάντα διὰ τοῦ ἐλέους σου καὶ κατὰ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

---

## Lutheran

In nomine Patris et Filii et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Adiutorium nostrum in nomine Domini,  
qui fecit caelum et terram.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum misericordiam tuam;  
secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.

Kyrie eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Credo in Deum Patrem omnipotentem, creatorem caeli et terrae.  
Et in Iesum Christum, Filium eius unicum, Dominum nostrum,  
qui conceptus est de Spiritu Sancto,  
natus ex Maria virgine,  
passus sub Pontio Pilato,  
crucifixus, mortuus, et sepultus,  
descendit ad inferos,  
tertia die resurrexit a mortuis,  
ascendit ad caelos,  
sedet ad dexteram Dei Patris omnipotentis,  
inde venturus est iudicare vivos et mortuos.  
Credo in Spiritum Sanctum,  
sanctam ecclesiam catholicam,  
sanctorum communionem,  
remissionem peccatorum,  
carnis resurrectionem,  
et vitam aeternam. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo.  
Amen.

Domine Deus, Pater caelestis,  
per Iesum Christum Filium tuum, Dominum nostrum,  
respice in misericordia super hoc opus fonte aperto.  
Non in meritis nostris confidimus,  
nec precationem nostram pretium aut commercium facimus,  
sed in sola misericordia tua et in promissione evangelii tui.

Da, quaesumus, ut hoc opus, si voluntati tuae congruit,  
diu floreat et recte serviat proximo;  
congrega cooperatores bonos, humiles, sapientes, et fideles in labore suo;  
auge benevolentiam, fiduciam, et utile testimonium inter eos qui hoc opus inveniunt;  
fac ut signa favoris et stellae aestimationis sponte et honeste accedant;  
custodi codicem ab errore noxio et ab vitio late serpente;  
concede diligentiam probandi, patientiam corrigendi,  
claritatem scribendi, et caritatem inter dissentientes.

Non petimus ut alii spolientur, minuantur, aut laedantur,  
sed ut dona tua recte dispensentur,  
et ut multi usores vera utilitate, pace, et bono communi fruantur.  
Averte superbiam, contentionem, fraudem, negligentiam,  
et omne malum quod fidei, caritati, et iusto operi nocet.

In manus tuas, Domine, commendamus hoc opus et omnes qui eo utuntur vel ei conferunt;  
redemisti nos, Domine Deus veritatis.

Benedicamus Domino.  
Deo gratias.

Benedicat nos omnipotens et misericors Dominus,  
Pater et Filius et Spiritus Sanctus. Amen.

---

## 摩门教（LDS）

Our Father in Heaven,

We thank Thee for the gifts of knowledge, cooperation, honest labor, and the opportunity to serve others through this open-source project.  
We acknowledge Thy Son, Jesus Christ, and seek the guidance of the Holy Ghost.

We ask Thee to bless this project with steady growth, faithful contributors, wise maintainers, helpful users, and increasing visibility among those who can benefit from it.  
Please help the code to be clear, reliable, well-reviewed, and protected from defects spreading unnoticed.  
May those who contribute do so with humility, patience, and charity; may those who use it receive real help; and may all labor be done without seeking to take from others, diminish their opportunities, or harm any life.

May Thy will be done, and may this work become a means of service, learning, and blessing according to faith in Jesus Christ.  
Please grant discernment, peace, and the companionship of the Holy Ghost to all who build, maintain, and benefit from it.

We say these things in the name of Jesus Christ, amen.

---

## 东正教 圣礼礼仪派

Εὐλογητὸς ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, πάντοτε, νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων.  
Ἀμήν.

Βασιλεῦ οὐράνιε, Παράκλητε, τὸ Πνεῦμα τῆς ἀληθείας, ὁ πανταχοῦ παρὼν καὶ τὰ πάντα πληρῶν, ὁ θησαυρὸς τῶν ἀγαθῶν καὶ ζωῆς χορηγός, ἐλθὲ καὶ σκήνωσον ἐν ἡμῖν, καὶ καθάρισον ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ πάσης κηλῖδος, καὶ σῶσον, Ἀγαθέ, τὰς ψυχὰς ἡμῶν.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

Παναγία Τριάς, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς· Κύριε, ἱλάσθητι ταῖς ἁμαρτίαις ἡμῶν· Δέσποτα, συγχώρησον τὰς ἀνομίας ἡμῖν· Ἅγιε, ἐπίσκεψαι καὶ ἴασαι τὰς ἀσθενείας ἡμῶν, ἕνεκεν τοῦ ὀνόματός σου.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς· ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου· ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου· γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου, ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς· τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον· καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν, ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφίεμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν· καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν, ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Ἐλέησόν με, ὁ Θεός, κατὰ τὸ μέγα ἔλεός σου, καὶ κατὰ τὸ πλῆθος τῶν οἰκτιρμῶν σου ἐξάλειψον τὸ ἀνόμημά μου.  
Ἐπὶ πλεῖον πλῦνόν με ἀπὸ τῆς ἀνομίας μου, καὶ ἀπὸ τῆς ἁμαρτίας μου καθάρισόν με.  
Ὅτι τὴν ἀνομίαν μου ἐγὼ γινώσκω, καὶ ἡ ἁμαρτία μου ἐνώπιόν μού ἐστι διὰ παντός.

Ἐν εἰρήνῃ τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς ἄνωθεν εἰρήνης καὶ τῆς σωτηρίας τῶν ψυχῶν ἡμῶν, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς εἰρήνης τοῦ σύμπαντος κόσμου, εὐσταθείας τῶν ἁγίων τοῦ Θεοῦ ἐκκλησιῶν, καὶ τῆς τῶν πάντων ἑνώσεως, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ ἔργου τούτου τοῦ ἀνοικτοῦ κώδικος, ἵνα ὁ Κύριος στερεώσῃ αὐτὸ ἐν ἀληθείᾳ, σοφίᾳ, διακρίσει καὶ ἀγάπῃ, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ μακροημερεύειν καὶ καρποφορεῖν τὸ ἔργον, καὶ συναχθῆναι συνεργοὺς ἀγαθοὺς, πραεῖς, συνετοὺς καὶ φιλαλλήλους, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ πληθυνθῆναι τὰ σημεῖα εὐμενείας καὶ οἱ ἀστέρες αὐτοῦ ἀβιάστως, μὴ ἀφαιρουμένων τῶν ἀγαθῶν τῶν πλησίον, μηδὲ βλαπτομένης ζωῆς ἢ κόπου ἑτέρου, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ φωτισθῆναι τὰς διανοίας τῶν γραφόντων, ἐξεταζόντων καὶ διορθούντων, ἵνα ὁ κώδιξ καθαρὸς γένηται, καὶ μὴ πλατυνθῶσι σφάλματα βλαπτικὰ ἐν αὐτῷ, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ πάντων τῶν χρηστών, ἵνα λάβωσιν ὠφέλειαν, εἰρήνην, ἀσφάλειαν καὶ καλὴν χρείαν, καὶ μηδεὶς σκανδαλισθῇ ἢ ζημιωθῇ, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ ῥυσθῆναι τὸ ἔργον ἀπὸ φιλονεικίας, κενοδοξίας, ἀμελείας, πλάνης, κινδύνου καὶ πάσης ἀνάγκης, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ἀντιλαβοῦ, σῶσον, ἐλέησον καὶ διαφύλαξον ἡμᾶς, ὁ Θεός, τῇ σῇ χάριτι.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὁ κατοικῶν ἐν βοηθείᾳ τοῦ Ὑψίστου, ἐν σκέπῃ τοῦ Θεοῦ τοῦ οὐρανοῦ αὐλισθήσεται.  
Ἐρεῖ τῷ Κυρίῳ· Ἀντιλήπτωρ μου εἶ καὶ καταφυγή μου, ὁ Θεός μου, καὶ ἐλπιῶ ἐπ’ αὐτόν.  
Ὅτι αὐτὸς ῥύσεταί σε ἐκ παγίδος θηρευτῶν καὶ ἀπὸ λόγου ταραχώδους.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ὁ φωτίζων πάντα ἄνθρωπον ἐρχόμενον εἰς τὸν κόσμον, κατάπεμψον τὴν εἰρηνικὴν σου χάριν ἐπὶ τὴν ἀγαθὴν ταύτην ἐπιχείρησιν· κυβέρνησον τὰ ἔργα τῶν χειρῶν καὶ τῶν νοῶν τῶν συνεργούντων, ἴθυνον τὰ βήματα αὐτῶν ἐν ταπεινώσει, καὶ ποίησον τὸν καρπὸν τοῦ κόπου κοινωφελῆ, ἀβλαβῆ καὶ εὐλογημένον, κατὰ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα.

Τῆς Παναγίας, ἀχράντου, ὑπερευλογημένης, ἐνδόξου Δεσποίνης ἡμῶν Θεοτόκου καὶ ἀειπαρθένου Μαρίας, μετὰ πάντων τῶν ἁγίων μνημονεύσαντες, ἑαυτοὺς καὶ ἀλλήλους καὶ πᾶσαν τὴν ζωὴν ἡμῶν Χριστῷ τῷ Θεῷ παραθώμεθα.  
Σοί, Κύριε.

Ὑπεραγία Θεοτόκε, σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Πάντες οἱ ἅγιοι, πρεσβεύσατε ὑπὲρ ἡμῶν.

Δόξα σοι, Χριστὲ ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἡ ἐλπὶς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Δι’ εὐχῶν τῶν ἁγίων Πατέρων ἡμῶν, Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἐλέησον καὶ σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἀμήν.

---

## Ritus Hispano-Mozarabicus

V. Dominus sit semper vobiscum.  
R. Et cum spiritu tuo.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Psalmus:  
Qui habitat in adiutorio Altissimi,  
in protectione Dei caeli commorabitur.  
Dicet Domino: Susceptor meus es tu et refugium meum;  
Deus meus, sperabo in eum.  
Quoniam ipse liberavit me de laqueo venantium,  
et a verbo aspero.  
Scapulis suis obumbrabit tibi,  
et sub pennis eius sperabis.

Lauda:  
Benedicite Dominum, omnes qui operamini veritatem;  
benedicite eum in scientia, in patientia et in caritate.  
Quoniam ipse dat sapientiam simplicibus,  
ordinat labores manuum nostrarum,  
et pacem tribuit omnibus qui bonum commune quaerunt.

Oratio admonitionis:  
Oremus, fratres carissimi, Dominum Deum omnipotentem,  
pro opere publico codicum aperto,  
ut idem opus diu floreat, utiliter crescat,  
contributores bonos, prudentes et concordes attrahat,  
signa favoris legitima sponte accipiat,  
codices eius ab erroribus noxiis et confusione serventur,  
et omnes qui eo utuntur fructum honestum, tutum et commune percipiant.

Non petimus, Domine, ut aliena auferantur,  
nec ut vita, salus, labor aut dignitas cuiusquam minuatur;  
sed ut quod iustum est, pacificum et utile,  
per misericordiam tuam augeatur.

R. Praesta, aeterne omnipotens Deus.

Alia:  
Deus, fons sapientiae et lumen mentium,  
qui artifices bonos donis Spiritus Sancti recreas,  
respice propitius super hoc opus apertum et commune.  
Da diligentiam scribentibus, humilitatem corrigentibus,  
patientiam probantibus, concordiam disceptantibus,  
et caritatem omnibus ministrantibus.  
Aufer ab eo vanam gloriam, contentionem, negligentiam et fraudem;  
revela errores latentes, sana vulnera codicum,  
confirma structuram, purifica intentionem,  
et dirige omnia ad verum servitium proximi.

R. Amen.

Post nomina:  
Memor esto, Domine, omnium viventium  
qui hoc opus mente, manu, consilio, tempore vel doctrina adiuvant;  
memor esto etiam omnium qui ex eius usu levamen, doctrinam, utilitatem  
vel instrumentum laboris honesti consequuntur.  
Et si qui ante nos in pace dormierunt,  
quorum scientia, exemplum vel labor viam praeparavit,  
dona eis locum refrigerii, lucis et pacis.

R. Amen.

Ad pacem:  
Pacem tuam, Domine Iesu Christe,  
quam dedisti discipulis tuis, conserva in nobis.  
Dissolve superbiam, comprime scandala,  
mitiga iracundiam, frange invidiam sine laesione personarum,  
et corda nostra in caritate tua confirma;  
ut qui diversa dona habent, unum bonum quaerant,  
et qui diversa munera gerunt, in uno Spiritu serviant.

R. Amen.

Sanctus:  
Sanctus, Sanctus, Sanctus Dominus Deus Sabaoth.  
Pleni sunt caeli et terra gloria tua.  
Hosanna in excelsis.  
Benedictus qui venit in nomine Domini.  
Hosanna in excelsis.

Pater noster:  
Pater noster, qui es in caelis:  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Completuria:  
Libera nos, Domine, ab omni malo,  
praeterito, praesenti et futuro;  
intercedente sancta et gloriosa Dei Genitrice Maria,  
cum beatis apostolis et omnibus sanctis,  
da propitius pacem in diebus nostris,  
ut ope misericordiae tuae adiuti  
et a peccato simus semper liberi  
et ab omni perturbatione securi.

Perfice, Domine, quod in nobis bonum est;  
quod pravum est corrige, quod fragile est confirma,  
quod obscurum est illumina, quod divisum est reconcilia.  
Sit hoc opus sub voluntate tua sancta,  
non ad iactantiam, non ad lucrum iniquum,  
sed ad communem utilitatem, doctrinam honestam,  
et servitium pacis.

R. Amen.

V. In nomine Domini nostri Iesu Christi perficiatur oratio nostra cum pace.  
R. Amen.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

---

## 新使徒改革

Father God, I come before You in the name of Jesus Christ concerning this open-source project and its appointed purpose.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Father, I confess and renounce every sin, pride, fear, rivalry, accusation, vanity, greed, confusion, careless stewardship, false word, and ungodly agreement connected with this work. I place this project under the blood and lordship of Jesus Christ.

I forgive all who have failed, misunderstood, criticized, delayed, or opposed this work, and I release them from my judgment. I do not curse them, control them, shame them, or claim vengeance over them. I bless what You bless, and I reject only the works of darkness, lies, bondage, sin, and oppression.

הַיֹּשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן  
בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי  
אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃

Ἰδοὺ δέδωκα ὑμῖν τὴν ἐξουσίαν  
τοῦ πατεῖν ἐπάνω ὄφεων καὶ σκορπίων,  
καὶ ἐπὶ πᾶσαν τὴν δύναμιν τοῦ ἐχθροῦ,  
καὶ οὐδὲν ὑμᾶς οὐ μὴ ἀδικήσει.

ὃ ἐὰν δήσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται δεδεμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς,  
καὶ ὃ ἐὰν λύσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται λελυμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς.

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ·  
ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ,  
καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I bind every demonic assignment, accusation, spirit of confusion, spirit of division, spirit of sabotage, spirit of fear, spirit of exploitation, destructive error, hidden vulnerability, malicious interference, and every power of the enemy operating against the righteous purpose of this project. I command every unclean influence attached to this work to leave and not return, according to the authority of Jesus Christ.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I loose truth, wisdom, humility, diligence, clean architecture, clear documentation, faithful maintainership, joyful contribution, wise review, timely correction, peaceful collaboration, righteous visibility, and lasting benefit over this project. Let contributors gather with goodwill; let stars come without manipulation; let bugs be found, contained, corrected, and not spread; let users receive real help, safety, and blessing through this work.

I cut off every ungodly tie to pride, competition, bitterness, burnout, confusion, manipulation, insecure dependency, corrupt motive, and unjust gain connected with this project. I declare that every hostile claim is canceled in Christ and that every power of darkness is disarmed under the cross of Jesus Christ.

Καὶ αὐτοὶ ἐνίκησαν αὐτὸν  
διὰ τὸ αἷμα τοῦ ἀρνίου  
καὶ διὰ τὸν λόγον τῆς μαρτυρίας αὐτῶν.

Father, fill every cleansed place with the Holy Spirit, the peace of Christ, the fear of the Lord, wisdom, purity, perseverance, creativity, and steadfast love. Establish Your kingdom order in the planning, code, review, release, community, governance, and use of this project.

I ask that this project may endure and flourish only according to Your will and righteousness. I do not seek to dispossess others, shorten anyone’s life, steal another’s honor, or gain success through another’s harm. Let every blessing received become service, integrity, and benefit for many.

Father, keep this prayer under the lordship, mercy, and holy will of Jesus Christ. Let my words be directed only against sin, bondage, lies, evil influence, unjust agreements, and the works of darkness, never against human persons or communities. If fear, compulsion, strife, or harm begins to arise, lead us away from aggressive speech and back into repentance, forgiveness, pastoral wisdom, peace, and fitting help. I thank You, Father, and seal this prayer in the name of Jesus Christ.

Ἀμήν.

---

## 贵格会（Quakers）

[Silence]

O God, Light within and beyond us,  
gather us into stillness.

The concern held before Thee is this open-source project:  
that it may endure in good order,  
that faithful contributors may gather freely,  
that recognition may come without vanity,  
that errors may be found and mended before they spread,  
and that all who use it may be helped.

We do not seek its flourishing by taking from another,  
nor by lessening the good, life, work, or peace of anyone else.  
Let truth, peace, mercy, and faithfulness be made plain.

The true Light:  
That was the true Light, which lighteth every man that cometh into the world.

If any of you lack wisdom, let him ask of God, that giveth to all men liberally, and upbraideth not; and it shall be given him.

Likewise the Spirit also helpeth our infirmities:  
for we know not what we should pray for as we ought:  
but the Spirit itself maketh intercession for us with groanings which cannot be uttered.  
And he that searcheth the hearts knoweth what is the mind of the Spirit,  
because he maketh intercession for the saints according to the will of God.

[Silence]

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

[Silence]

If words are given:

Lord, make us faithful in this work.  
Keep its makers and users in Thy Light.  
Guide what must be written,  
still what must not be rushed,  
reveal what is broken,  
heal what may be healed,  
release what must be released,  
and order each contribution in peace.

May the project serve rather than dominate,  
invite rather than compel,  
and remain open to correction, generosity, and truth.

[Silence]

---

## старообрядцы

Во имя Отца и Сына и Святаго Духа. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй мя грешнаго.

Царю Небесныи, Утешителю, Душе истинныи, иже везде сыи и вся исполняя, сокровище благих и жизни подателю, прииди и вселися в ны, и очисти ны от всякия скверны, и спаси, Блаже, душа наша.

Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Пресвятая Троице, помилуй нас. Господи, очисти грехи наша. Владыко, прости беззакония наша. Святыи, посети и исцели немощи наша, имене Твоего ради.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Отче наш, иже еси на небесех, да святится имя Твое, да приидет Царствие Твое, да будет воля Твоя, яко на небеси и на земли. Хлеб наш насущныи даждь нам днесь, и остави нам долги наша, якоже и мы оставляем должником нашим, и не введи нас во искушение, но избави нас от лукаваго.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Верую во единаго Бога Отца, Вседержителя, Творца небу и земли, видимым же всем и невидимым. И во единаго Господа Исуса Христа, Сына Божия, Единороднаго, иже от Отца рожденнаго прежде всех век. Света от Света, Бога истинна от Бога истинна, рожденна, а не сотворенна, единосущна Отцу, Имже вся быша. Нас ради человек и нашего ради спасения сшедшаго с небес, и воплотившагося от Духа Свята и Марии Девы, и вочеловечшася. Распятаго же за ны при Понтийстем Пилате, и страдавша, и погребенна. И воскресшаго в третии день по Писанием. И возшедшаго на небеса, и седяща одесную Отца. И паки грядущаго со славою судити живым и мертвым, Его же Царствию несть конца. И в Духа Святаго, Господа истиннаго и животворящаго, иже от Отца исходящаго, иже со Отцем и Сыном спокланяема и сславима, глаголавшаго пророки. Во едину святую соборную и апостольскую Церковь. Исповедую едино крещение во оставление грехов. Чаю воскресения мертвым, и жизни будущаго века. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, призри милостивно на дело сие общеполезное, на писание исхода отверстаго и на трудящихся в нем: подаждь им разум чист, совет благ, терпение, мир и любовь нелицемерну.

Благослови, Владыко, да пребудет дело сие долго и непоколебимо, да соберутся к нему помощницы и делатели добрыя, да умножится благоволение к нему без тщеславия, да исправятся погрешения писания и да не распространится вред и смущение, но да будет польза всем, иже сего труда касаются.

Не просим, Господи, отъяти чужий жребий, ни лишити кого труда и достатка, ни умалити живота или блага инаго человека; но просим честнаго успеха, мира, правды, исправления и пользы, аще есть сие угодно святей воле Твоей.

Помилуй мя, Боже, по велицей милости Твоей, и по множеству щедрот Твоих очисти беззаконие мое. Наипаче омый мя от беззакония моего, и от греха моего очисти мя.

Живыи в помощи Вышняго, в крове Бога Небеснаго водворится. Речет Господеви: Заступник мой еси и Прибежище мое, Бог мой, и уповаю на Него.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.

Пресвятая Богородице, спаси нас.

Достойно есть яко воистинну блажити Тя, Богородицу, присноблаженную и пренепорочную и Матерь Бога нашего. Честнейшую херувим и славнейшую воистинну серафим, без истления Бога Слова рождшую, сущую Богородицу Тя величаем.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, не по страстем нашим, но по святей воле Твоей устрой вся ко спасению и ко пользе ближних; молитв ради Пречистыя Твоея Матере и всех святых, помилуй и спаси нас, яко Благ и Человеколюбец. Аминь.
